The company is also taking over the debt of Swal amounting to Rs 4 crore.',  The deal, which was finalised on Wednesday, enables UPL to become a market leader in some key segments of the agrochemical industry. The Jumbo group has exited the business as part of its strategy to exit non-core areas. While the Jumbo group was advised by Mumbai-based Singhi & Associates advisors, Yes Bank was the sole advisor for United Phosphorus.', u" UPL is funding the transaction through its internal cash accruals. Swal, which has a turnover of Rs 70 crore, has a manufacturing plant located in Haldia which manufactures the active ingredient for the agrochemical industry. Swal's present activities include manufacturing, formulation and marketing of agrochemicals and fertiliser mixtures.", u" The acquisition will give UPL increased access in markets like AP, Maharashtra, Kerala and Tamil Nadu. Under the deal, around 100 employees will be integrated into UPL. ET had earlier reported that UPL is in talks to takeover Swal's agrochem business.", u" Swal has seen a major turnaround with turnover increasing from Rs 23.3 crores in '01-02 to Rs 75 crores in '04-05. During this period, it has also revamped its operations with special emphasis on product rationalisation, manpower and operating expense control, leading to its net profit increasing to Rs 4.5 crores in '04-05 against a peak net loss of Rs.5.17 crore in '02-03.",  During this period, the company has doubled its market share in its two main products, namely, Acephate and Ethion. The company has a strong product pipeline and is working on expanding its product range.', u" This is UPL's second acquisition in this financial year following its takeover of CEQUISA, a Spanish agchem company with 400 registrations worldwide and sales of Euro19.3m (Rs 106 crores). Besides, in November '04, UPL has also acquired Agvalue in the US making it third acquisition in the last 12 months.", u" UPL is one the largest Indian agrochemical players which is engaged in research, manufacture and distribution of agrochemicals and speciality chemicals across the globe. The company's revenue's for the year ending March '05 were in excess of Rs 1,422 crores.",  Through strategic alliances and network of over 20 subsidiaries, UPL has built a marketing network across the globe and its international revenues account for over 70% of its total revenues. It exports to over 100 countries, the primary markets being Europe and North America.',  ', See more', See more', We are the leading global producer and exporter of crop protection and post-harvest agriculture chemicals. The company is also taking over the debt of Swal amounting to Rs 4 crore.',  The deal, which was finalised on Wednesday, enables UPL to become a market leader in some key segments of the agrochemical industry. The Jumbo group has exited the business as part of its strategy to exit non-core areas. While the Jumbo group was advised by Mumbai-based Singhi & Associates advisors, Yes Bank was the sole advisor for United Phosphorus.', u" UPL is funding the transaction through its internal cash accruals. Swal, which has a turnover of Rs 70 crore, has a manufacturing plant located in Haldia which manufactures the active ingredient for the agrochemical industry. Swal's present activities include manufacturing, formulation and marketing of agrochemicals and fertiliser mixtures.", u" The acquisition will give UPL increased access in markets like AP, Maharashtra, Kerala and Tamil Nadu. Under the deal, around 100 employees will be integrated into UPL. ET had earlier reported that UPL is in talks to takeover Swal's agrochem business.", u" Swal has seen a major turnaround with turnover increasing from Rs 23.3 crores in '01-02 to Rs 75 crores in '04-05. During this period, it has also revamped its operations with special emphasis on product rationalisation, manpower and operating expense control, leading to its net profit increasing to Rs 4.5 crores in '04-05 against a peak net loss of Rs.5.17 crore in '02-03.",  During this period, the company has doubled its market share in its two main products, namely, Acephate and Ethion. The company has a strong product pipeline and is working on expanding its product range.', u" This is UPL's second acquisition in this financial year following its takeover of CEQUISA, a Spanish agchem company with 400 registrations worldwide and sales of Euro19.3m (Rs 106 crores).
